4. **11Q13 (Melchizedek Scroll)** — Melchizedek as a divine figure who executes judgment on the fallen gods of Psalm 82. Connects Gen 14 to Ps 82 to Ps 110 to Hebrews 7.
5. **Great Isaiah Scroll (1QIsa^a)** — Complete Isaiah text confirming textual integrity.

---

### ENOCH & THE DIVINE COUNCIL (Deep Dive)
**Era files**: 4 (era_walked_with_god, era_throne_vision, era_council_pattern, era_mediator)
**Position**: App-specific study exploring Enoch's role as council intercessor

Traces Enoch as the human who walked with God (Gen 5:24), witnessed the divine throne, observed the council pattern across Scripture, and served as mediator between heaven and earth — prefiguring Christ's own mediatorial role.

---

### THEMATIC STUDY COLLECTIONS

These are interpretive frameworks built into the app that trace threads across the entire canon:

- **Three Rebellions** (4 eras) — Eden (nachash), Hermon (200 Watchers), Babel (nations allotted to lesser gods), plus the three reversals through Christ (Cross, Proclamation to spirits, Pentecost)
- **Messianic Thread** (3 eras) — Traces the seed promise from Gen 3:15 through the patriarchs, the prophets, and into fulfillment in Christ
- **Nephilim & Giants** (3 eras) — Origin in Gen 6, survival through the Flood (Num 13, Deut 2-3, Amos 2:9), David's final eradication of the giant clans
- **Parables Invitation** (3 eras) — Jesus' parable theology: the wedding invitation, the mystery of the kingdom, faith vs. theology
- **Canon & Scripture** (3 eras) — How the OT and NT canons formed, canonical traditions across church history
- **Canon & Septuagint** (5 eras) — LXX vs. MT, DSS confirmation of older readings, the 1 Enoch tradition, other non-canonical texts
- **Church History** (4 eras) — Apostolic age through the Reformation, tracing how theological understanding shifted

---

## FINAL SUMMARY — THE STORY ARC

The entire Bible tells ONE story in five acts:

1. **CREATION & REBELLION** (Gen 1-11): God creates, the council exists, three rebellions fracture creation — Eden (nachash), Hermon (200 Watchers), Babel (nations allotted to lesser gods under Deut 32:8).

2. **COVENANT & PROMISE** (Gen 12 - Malachi): God calls Abraham, builds a nation, gives Torah, establishes David's throne, sends prophets as covenant prosecutors. But Israel cannot keep the covenant — exile proves the anthropological problem. The prophets promise a new covenant, a suffering servant, a divine son of man, a Spirit outpouring.

3. **INCARNATION & VICTORY** (Gospels): The divine Son — member of the council from before creation (John 1:1, 17:5) — enters creation as human. He defeats the nachash's temptation (Matt 4), casts out demons (reclaiming territory), teaches the kingdom, dies on the cross (Col 2:15 — disarming the powers), rises from the dead (defeating death itself), and ascends to the right hand (Ps 110:1 fulfilled).

4. **RECLAMATION & MISSION** (Acts - Jude): The Spirit falls at Pentecost (Babel reversed). The ekklesia — not a building but a governing assembly — carries the gospel to every nation, reclaiming what was allotted to lesser gods. The apostles teach the cosmic scope: principalities and powers are real, the warfare is spiritual, and the victory is already won.

5. **RESTORATION & NEW CREATION** (Revelation): The nachash is finally identified (Rev 12:9), judged, and destroyed. The nations are healed (22:2). Eden is restored — river of life, tree of life, God dwelling with humanity. The council's work is complete. The kingdom is YHWH's.

**Genesis 3:15 is the thesis statement. Revelation 22 is the conclusion. Everything between is that verse playing out.**

---

## APPENDIX A: How to Read This Index

- Each book analysis follows the same template
- Theme codes (SEED, COV, DC, etc.) let you trace a thread across ALL books
- Outlier flags help identify which books break patterns and WHY
- Contested words accumulate into a master glossary
- Gaps become our development roadmap

---

## APPENDIX B: Family Trees & Peoples of Genesis-Exodus

Map out EVERY family line and people group traceable in Genesis and Exodus. Include:

### The Seed Line (Adam → Israel)
Adam → Seth → Enosh → Kenan → Mahalalel → Jared → Enoch → Methuselah → Lamech → Noah → Shem → Arpachshad → Shelah → Eber → Peleg → Reu → Serug → Nahor → Terah → ABRAHAM → Isaac → Jacob/Israel → 12 Tribes

### The Anti-Seed / Rival Lines
- Cain's line: Cain → Enoch (different from Seth's Enoch) → Irad → Mehujael → Methushael → Lamech (the bigamist/murderer, Gen 4:23-24) — LINE ENDS at the Flood
- Ishmael's line: 12 princes (Gen 25:12-18) — becomes Arab peoples
- Esau's line: Edom/Edomites (Gen 36) — perpetual rivals of Israel, Herod the Great was Idumean (Edomite)

### Table of Nations (Genesis 10)
- Japheth's sons: Gomer, Magog, Madai, Javan, Tubal, Meshech, Tiras → European/Anatolian/Iranian peoples
- Ham's sons: Cush, Mizraim (Egypt), Put, Canaan → African/Canaanite peoples. Nimrod from Cush (first empire builder, Babel/Nineveh). Canaan's sons = the peoples Israel displaces
- Shem's sons: Elam, Asshur, Arpachshad, Lud, Aram → Mesopotamian/Semitic peoples. Abraham descends through Arpachshad.

### Jacob's 12 Sons (Tribal Origins)
By Leah: Reuben, Simeon, Levi, Judah, Issachar, Zebulun (+ Dinah)
By Rachel: Joseph (→ Ephraim + Manasseh), Benjamin
By Bilhah (Rachel's servant): Dan, Naphtali
By Zilpah (Leah's servant): Gad, Asher

Note which tribes have special significance:
- JUDAH — messianic/royal line (Gen 49:10 "the scepter shall not depart")
- LEVI — priestly tribe (chosen after golden calf, Ex 32)
- JOSEPH (Ephraim/Manasseh) — double portion, dominant northern tribe
- BENJAMIN — smallest tribe, later produces Saul, Paul

### Peoples Encountered
- Philistines (Caphtorim from Crete/Aegean via Ham)
- Moabites (from Lot + elder daughter, Gen 19:37)
- Ammonites (from Lot + younger daughter, Gen 19:38)
- Midianites (from Abraham + Keturah, Gen 25:2)
- Amalekites (from Esau's grandson Amalek, Gen 36:12 — Israel's perpetual enemy)
- Hittites (from Canaan's son Heth)
- Kenites (connected to Cain? Jethro's people)

### Key Marriages That Shape History
- Abraham + Sarah → Isaac (covenant line)
- Abraham + Hagar → Ishmael (Arab peoples)
- Abraham + Keturah → Midian and others
- Isaac + Rebekah → Jacob + Esau
- Jacob + Leah/Rachel/Bilhah/Zilpah → 12 tribes
- Judah + Tamar → Perez → David → Jesus
- Joseph + Asenath (Egyptian priest's daughter) → Ephraim + Manasseh

### The Nephilim / Giant Clans (tracked from Gen 6)
- Nephilim (Gen 6:4) — pre-flood, offspring of bene ha'elohim + human women
- Nephilim in Canaan (Num 13:33) — post-flood, spies report "sons of Anak who come from the Nephilim"
- Anakim (Deut 2:10-11) — "great and tall," considered Rephaim
- Rephaim (Gen 14:5, 15:20, Deut 2:11) — ancient giant clan in Transjordan
- Emim (Deut 2:10) — Moab's name for the Rephaim in their territory
- Zamzummim (Deut 2:20) — Ammon's name for the Rephaim in their territory
- Og of Bashan (Deut 3:11) — last of the Rephaim, bed was 13.5 feet long
- Goliath and his brothers (1 Sam 17, 2 Sam 21:15-22) — Philistine giants, possible last Nephilim remnant
NOTE: This connects to our Nephilim & Giants thematic study (3 era files)

---

## APPENDIX C: Geography & Map Integration Guide

### Genesis Key Locations (App Map Opportunities)

**Primeval History (Gen 1-11)**
- Eden — location debated: Tigris/Euphrates confluence (southern Iraq), Armenia (headwaters), or symbolic
- Land of Nod — "east of Eden" (Gen 4:16), unknown
- Ararat — mountains where ark landed (Gen 8:4), modern eastern Turkey/Armenia
- Babel/Shinar — southern Mesopotamia, later Babylon (modern Iraq)
- Ur of the Chaldees — southern Mesopotamia (modern Tell el-Muqayyar, Iraq) — Abraham's origin

**Patriarchal Routes (Gen 12-50)**
1. Abraham's Journey: Ur → Haran → Shechem → Bethel → Negev → Egypt → Negev → Hebron → Mount Moriah → Beer-sheba
2. Jacob's Journey: Beer-sheba → Bethel (ladder dream) → Haran (20 years) → Mahanaim → Peniel (wrestling) → Shechem → Bethel → Hebron
3. Joseph's Journey: Hebron → Dothan (sold) → Egypt (Potiphar's house → prison → palace → Goshen)

**Key Sites**
- Shechem — first place Abraham stops in Canaan, first altar (Gen 12:6-7)
- Bethel — Jacob's ladder, renamed from Luz (Gen 28:19)
- Hebron/Mamre — Abraham's main residence, burial cave (Machpelah) (Gen 13:18, 23:19)
- Beer-sheba — "well of the oath," southern boundary marker (Gen 21:31)
- Mount Moriah — the binding of Isaac (Gen 22) = Temple Mount (2 Chr 3:1)
- Sodom/Gomorrah — Dead Sea region, destroyed (Gen 19)
- Goshen — northeast Nile Delta, Israel's settlement in Egypt

### Exodus Key Locations

**Egypt**
- Goshen / Land of Rameses — northeast Nile Delta
- Pithom (Tell el-Retabeh or Tell el-Maskhuta) — store city
- Pi-Ramesses (Qantir) — Pharaoh's capital in the Delta

**Exodus Route (debated)**
- Rameses → Succoth → Etham → sea crossing (yam suph, location contested)
- Northern route: along the Mediterranean coast (Way of Horus) — BUT Ex 13:17 says God did NOT lead them this way
- Central route: through the Bitter Lakes region
- Southern route: down the Sinai Peninsula to Jebel Musa
- Arabian route: crossing Gulf of Aqaba to Jebel al-Lawz in Midian

**Wilderness Sites**
- Marah — bitter water made sweet
- Elim — 12 springs, 70 palm trees
- Wilderness of Sin — manna begins
- Rephidim — water from rock, Amalek battle
- Mount Sinai/Horeb — THE mountain (location debated: Jebel Musa traditional; Jebel al-Lawz alternative)

### How to Add to the App Map System

Reference the existing map journey system in the app:
- Journey routes are defined in `data/{book}/info.py` under a `journeys` key or in the BOOK_TO_JOURNEYS mapping in app.js
- Each journey has waypoints with lat/lng coordinates, descriptions, and verse references
- The map uses Leaflet.js with custom markers

**Suggested new map routes to build:**
1. "Abraham's Journey" — Ur to Canaan (already may exist, verify)
2. "Jacob's Journey" — Beer-sheba to Haran and back
3. "Joseph to Egypt" — Dothan to Egypt
4. "The Exodus Route" — Egypt to Sinai (with alternative route options)
5. "Table of Nations" — Fan-out from Babel showing where Japheth/Ham/Shem peoples settled
6. "The Nephilim Geography" — Where giant clans are reported across Canaan and Transjordan

**Data format for map journeys** (check existing journey files for exact format):
```python
JOURNEYS = [
    {
        "id": "abraham_journey",
        "name": "Abraham's Journey to Canaan",
        "color": "#DAA520",
        "waypoints": [
            {"name": "Ur of the Chaldees", "lat": 30.96, "lng": 46.10, "ref": "Gen 11:31", "desc": "Abraham's origin city"},
            {"name": "Haran", "lat": 36.87, "lng": 39.03, "ref": "Gen 11:31", "desc": "Terah settles here; Abraham called to leave"},
            # ... etc
        ]
    }
]
```
